# Simulation Base Information:
+ Population: 1000
+ Percent Population Vaccinated: 0.2
+ Virus Name: Sniffles
+ Virus Mortality Rate: 0.12
+ Virus Reproduction Rate: 0.5
```diff
! create_population() !
+ Vaccinated : 200
+ Unvaccinated : 750
+ Infected : 50
```
